Dirty-Frame Reflow Scheduling\\n\\n`PresShell::FrameNeedsReflow` (PresShell.cpp:2632) marks the frame and its ancestors with dirty bits (`NS_FRAME_IS_DIRTY` or `NS_FRAME_HAS_DIRTY_CHILDREN`), propagating up to the nearest reflow root, and adds the frame to `mDirtyRoots`.\\n\\nReflow is executed by `PresShell::DoFlushLayout` (line 10716) → `PresShell::ProcessReflowCommands` (line 10637), which pops dirty roots from `mDirtyRoots` and calls `DoReflow()` for each. Display List Construction\\n\\nAfter reflow, the refresh driver's `PaintIfNeeded` (nsRefreshDriver.cpp:2598) calls `PresShell::PaintSynchronously` (PresShell.cpp:12326) → `PresShell::PaintAndRequestComposite` (line 6421) → `PresShell::PaintInternal` (line 6467), which calls `nsLayoutUtils::PaintFrame` (nsLayoutUtils.cpp:2834).\\n\\n`nsLayoutUtils::PaintFrame` constructs the display list:\\n- For retained/partial builds: `RetainedDisplayListBuilder::AttemptPartialUpdate` (layout/painting/RetainedDisplayListBuilder.cpp:1565) attempts an incremental update of the retained display list by calling `BuildDisplayListForStackingContext` only on modified subtrees.\\n- For full builds: `nsIFrame::BuildDisplayListForStackingContext` is called directly on the root frame.\\n- The completed display list is then passed to `nsDisplayList::PaintRoot` (layout/painting/nsDisplayList.cpp:2348).\\n\\n## 5. WebRender Layer Update\\n\\n`nsDisplayList::PaintRoot` invokes `WebRenderLayerManager::EndTransactionWithoutLayer` (gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderLayerManager.cpp:338), which:\\n- Calls `WebRenderCommandBuilder::BuildWebRenderCommands` (gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderCommandBuilder.cpp:1755) to translate the Gecko display list items into WebRender display list primitives (via `CreateWebRenderCommandsFromDisplayList`).\\n- Calls `wr::DisplayListBuilder::End()` to finalize the WR display list.\\n- Sends the display list to the compositor process via `WebRenderBridgeChild::SendSetDisplayList` (gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderBridgeChild.cpp:139), which is an IPC message.\\n\\nOn the compositor side, `WebRenderBridgeParent::RecvSetDisplayList` (gfx/layers/wr/WebRenderBridgeParent.cpp:1325) receives the message and calls `ProcessDisplayListData` (line 1273), which forwards the display list to WebRender's scene builder thread via `SetDisplayList()`. WebRender then asynchronously builds a new scene, rasterizes, and composites the result to the screen.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
